# Supported Protocols | Kiln docs

Partners can choose any asset available to supply on the supported protocols and chains below.

circle-info

All ERC-20 tokens available on the integrated protocols are supported by Kiln DeFi.

However, native tokens are not supported (i.e. ETH), while the ERC-20 wrapped versions are (i.e. WETH, WBTC)

For each unique '_protocol <> asset <> chain_' combination, a dedicated vault is deployed for the integration.

_For example, if an partner wants to create a strategy around USDC on Ethereum mainnet for AAVE v3, Compound v3, and on Base for Compound v3, then 3 vaults will be deployed:_

*   _USDC <> Aave v3 <> Ethereum_
    
*   _USDC <> Compound v3 <> Ethereum_
    
*   _USDC <> Compound v3 <> Base_
    

**Supported protocols, assets and chains**

Please be aware that assets with negligible Total Value Locked (TVL) or minimal yield generation are not listed in our documentation for convenience. We aim to update this page on a monthly basis so the details below may change.

For the latest information, you can always access the lending protocol directly through the links provided below or you can use [this linkarrow-up-right](https://defillama.com/yields?project=aave-v3&project=morpho-aave&project=compound-v3&project=morpho-compound&project=morpho-blue&project=sdai&project=venus-core-pool&project=spark&project=angle&project=frax&project=fluid&project=zerolend&project=makerdao&project=kinetic&minTvl=1000000&maxTvl=&attribute=single_exposure&attribute=no_il)
 that provides a single view of all protocols and asset yield.

We are always evaluating new DeFi protocols to support, and can quickly add new protocols based on demand. Adding support for additional EVM-based chains is generally quick and easy. We are also exploring support for select non-EVM chains, such as Tron and Solana. If your preferred DeFi protocol or blockchain is not listed here, please contact us to discuss its addition.

Protocol (11)

Supported Chains

# Injective (INJ) | Kiln docs

![](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1911902555-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fnye3yqpuOzdfrtWAlwng%252Fuploads%252F32akoh0ZEbg7X5fprdCf%252FScreenshot%25202024-08-28%2520at%252007.02.54.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5de60d73-0458-4cba-810b-5ca5eb38715e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b86bf91f&sv=2)

INJ stakes

[hashtag](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/kiln-products/dashboard/unstaking/injective-inj#unstake)

Unstake


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can unstake INJ by simply clicking "Unstake" on your stake. After that you will be able to connect your Fireblocks Vault and unstake your INJ.

Please keep in mind that the unstaked INJ becomes unbonding and you will need to wait for 21 days before you can use those INJ again.

![](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1911902555-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fnye3yqpuOzdfrtWAlwng%252Fuploads%252FCYmkeTiEfGVhzHq3gDrY%252FScreenshot%25202024-08-28%2520at%252007.13.43.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D50dbcd30-822d-4db8-a544-c7949b461f24&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=38659c16&sv=2)

Unstake INJ

[hashtag](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/kiln-products/dashboard/unstaking/injective-inj#re-delegate)

Re-delegate


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Re-delegating an INJ stake can be useful when you wish to move your staked INJ to a different validator without waiting for the 21 days unbonding period happening when unstaking.

This can be done by selecting "Re-delegate" for an INJ stake on the dashboard and specifying a new validator.

![](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1911902555-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fnye3yqpuOzdfrtWAlwng%252Fuploads%252F3Dxj2iLOOjfVVb6phi7H%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D34d647cd-db8e-4d07-ad1a-b764a700a44e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=904ac7a&sv=2)

INJ Re-delegate is the same experience that ATOM

[hashtag](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/kiln-products/dashboard/unstaking/injective-inj#withdraw-rewards)

Withdraw rewards


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can withdraw your available INJ rewards, by selecting "Withdraw rewards" on the dashboard. After that you will be able to connect your Fireblocks Vault and withdraw your INJ rewards.

![](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1911902555-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fnye3yqpuOzdfrtWAlwng%252Fuploads%252FSL4IWvWcAqPwtYkdcddG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D289aeee9-851e-42d9-aa60-abbfcda1c0d2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6e24b0f8&sv=2)

Withdraw INJ available rewards is the same experience than ATOM

[PreviousFetch.ai (FET)chevron-left](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/kiln-products/dashboard/unstaking/fetch.ai-fet)
[NextKusama (KSM)chevron-right](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/kiln-products/dashboard/unstaking/kusama-ksm)

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Unstake](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/kiln-products/dashboard/unstaking/injective-inj#unstake)
    
*   [Re-delegate](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/kiln-products/dashboard/unstaking/injective-inj#re-delegate)
    
*   [Withdraw rewards](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/kiln-products/dashboard/unstaking/injective-inj#withdraw-rewards)
    

Was this helpful?

# Tron (TRX) | Kiln docs

![](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1911902555-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fnye3yqpuOzdfrtWAlwng%252Fuploads%252FJujLkkXRWnEZOhPS5zqt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcbc9f623-ec73-41c2-bfac-3249604a7f1d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a3bab94d&sv=2)

TRX stakes on Kiln Dashboard

[hashtag](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/kiln-products/dashboard/unstaking/tron-trx#unstake)

Unstake


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can unstake TRX by simply clicking "Unstake" on your stake. After that you will be able to connect your wallet and unstake.

circle-exclamation

After unstaking, you need to wait for 14 days before being able to withdraw the funds of this unstaking.

If there are previously unstaked assets that have passed the lock-up period, this unstaking operation will automatically withdraw them to the account.

![](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1911902555-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fnye3yqpuOzdfrtWAlwng%252Fuploads%252FcJb1NBkhgy9wEjp6sKto%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D32e995cd-9ce7-4fb2-9700-3eea59ec338f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6f3488a0&sv=2)

Unstake TRX on Kiln Dashboard

[hashtag](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/kiln-products/dashboard/unstaking/tron-trx#withdraw-rewards)

Withdraw rewards


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can withdraw your available TRX rewards, by selecting "Withdraw rewards" on the dashboard. After that you will be able to connect your Fireblocks Vault and withdraw your TRX rewards.

![](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1911902555-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fnye3yqpuOzdfrtWAlwng%252Fuploads%252F0ONydWhfXfGlf3e0Jat0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddf3f14e6-42c5-47ff-9c5b-33c263317252&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a0485e85&sv=2)

Withdraw TRX rewards

[PreviousTezos (XTZ)chevron-left](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/kiln-products/dashboard/unstaking/tezos-xtz)
[NextThe Open Network (TON)chevron-right](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/kiln-products/dashboard/unstaking/the-open-network-ton)

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Unstake](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/kiln-products/dashboard/unstaking/tron-trx#unstake)
    
*   [Withdraw rewards](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/kiln-products/dashboard/unstaking/tron-trx#withdraw-rewards)
    

Was this helpful?

# Smart Contract interaction | Kiln docs

**We DO NOT recommend you proceed with this path unless you are an experienced user and have an urgent need to access the funds.**

**Please be aware of scam, if you are not sure about something, ask** [Support](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/working-with-kiln/support)
**, or wait for your prefered UI to be back online.**

**Note: If you are trying to interact with the contract via a Ledger device, Ledger Live does not work currently. We would recommend you connect it with a trusted browser wallet extension, for example Rabby Wallet or Trust Wallet. See** [**here**arrow-up-right](https://support.ledger.com/article/4409801559569-zd)
 **for more info.**

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/kiln-products/omnivaults/smart-contract-interaction#view-your-position-via-etherscan)

View your position via Etherscan

1.  Open your wallet address on Etherscan:
    
    1.  eg. [https://etherscan.io/address/0x2eec5d4dcbb5c15a7924b54e6cb516a6bb0a1c3farrow-up-right](https://etherscan.io/address/0x2eec5d4dcbb5c15a7924b54e6cb516a6bb0a1c3f)
        
    
2.  Click on token holdings and over the ERC-20 to see names related to your preferred application, it will open the holder history filtered on your wallet, where you can find all transaction you did for this defi product.
    
    ![](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1911902555-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fnye3yqpuOzdfrtWAlwng%252Fuploads%252F83nyJ4cGTRbDAuxpSbQP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc9057bf3-54b0-4bf1-9b98-b4a3c7fdfa03&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a5f66a26&sv=2)
    
    1.  You can already see here the amount you hold, here
        
        1.  3136.22 `cwAaveUSDT`
            
        
    
3.  On the transaction page, over the Interacted With (To) address and click on it.
    
    1.  Eg. [https://etherscan.io/address/0x924e38bdfda04990fc78fec258e8b83b3478b1af#codearrow-up-right](https://etherscan.io/address/0x924e38bdfda04990fc78fec258e8b83b3478b1af#code)
        
    2.  ![](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1911902555-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fnye3yqpuOzdfrtWAlwng%252Fuploads%252F1YKSPzxypFdc5a0mdknR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deac4807f-9198-48b6-b973-da61d94301c9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=79bb4a02&sv=2)
        
    
4.  On the deposit contract page, navigate to the `Contract` tab and sub tab `Read as Proxy` , find `31. maxRedeem (0xd905777e)`
    
    1.  Input your wallet address, and click **query.**
        
    2.  eg. for `0x2eEC5D4dcBB5C15A7924b54E6CB516A6BB0A1C3F` it returns: `3136221376` it's the amount in USDT your principal + rewards is worth.
        
    3.  To see this amount in a human readable format, read the `19. decimals (0x313ce567)` function on the same page.
        
        1.  eg. for this defi position I receive `6` `decimals`
            
        2.  You can then multiply the maxRedeem value `3136221376` to 1e-`decimals` , so here `3136221376``*1e-``6` = `3 136,221376`
            
        
    4.  To confirm the asset read the `11. asset (0x38d52e0f)` function on the same page, and click on the asset address, you will see the asset deposited in this defi position here. `USDT`.
        
        1.  ![](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1911902555-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fnye3yqpuOzdfrtWAlwng%252Fuploads%252FfZ9nbHDTjPldzBFPG6Dw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc7aeeb31-4b93-4c16-8516-1b5123be271e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a83048b9&sv=2)
            
        
    5.  Doing so I can confirm that I own and can redeem anytime `3 136,221376 USDT`
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/kiln-products/omnivaults/smart-contract-interaction#withdraw-all-assets-deposited-aka-redeem-via-etherscan)

Withdraw all assets deposited aka Redeem via Etherscan

_Requirement, connnect you wallet to a browser wallet or use Wallet Connect to connect to Etherscan._

In this example we show how you can **withdraw all your asset from your position** in Etherscan.

1.  Find the defi position deposit contract (see [View your position via Etherscan](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/kiln-products/omnivaults/smart-contract-interaction#view-your-position-via-etherscan)
    )
    
    1.  eg. [https://etherscan.io/address/0x924e38bdfda04990fc78fec258e8b83b3478b1af#codearrow-up-right](https://etherscan.io/address/0x924e38bdfda04990fc78fec258e8b83b3478b1af#code)
        
    
2.  On the deposit contract page, navigate to the `Contract` tab and sub tab `Read as Proxy` , find `12.balanceOf 0x70a08231)`
    
    1.  Past your wallet address and click **query**.
        
    2.  eg. for `0x2eEC5D4dcBB5C15A7924b54E6CB516A6BB0A1C3F` , it's `3136221376` , this is the amount of shared you own, it's representing your principal + all rewards.
        
    
3.  On the deposit contract page, navigate to the `Contract` tab and sub tab `Write as Proxy` , find `16.redeem (0xba087652)`
    
    1.  Input the value you got from the previous `balanceOf` read on step 2, and your wallet for `receiver` and `owner` . (Make sure you connect your wallet on top)
        
        1.  ![](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1911902555-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fnye3yqpuOzdfrtWAlwng%252Fuploads%252F3v9kvrxt419mRHMdPEyo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcd0373ab-d38f-491c-acd4-0f7f347c35b3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=334056af&sv=2)
            
        
    2.  You will be prompted in your wallet to sign the transaction.
        
        ![](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1911902555-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fnye3yqpuOzdfrtWAlwng%252Fuploads%252FbMauopPjkpO7oTgUwsRh%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D43b729c6-5cb5-4418-8db3-7967d030b517&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1442a97f&sv=2)
        
    
4.  After signing this one transaction you will directly receive the assets directly in your wallet.

# Fetch.ai (FET) | Kiln docs

![](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1911902555-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fnye3yqpuOzdfrtWAlwng%252Fuploads%252Fs0y0l0hwV2I9j9CecFWQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D72766b33-850d-4f42-a8a6-1efd80c4ec3a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=56a31712&sv=2)

FET stakes

[hashtag](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/kiln-products/dashboard/unstaking/fetch.ai-fet#unstake)

Unstake


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can unstake FET by simply clicking "Unstake" on your stake. After that you will be able to connect your Fireblocks Vault and unstake your FET.

Please keep in mind that the unstaked FET becomes unbonding and you will need to wait for 21 days before you can use those FET again.

![](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1911902555-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fnye3yqpuOzdfrtWAlwng%252Fuploads%252FqX1eUuXHff67XPllQAop%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc55e99ac-7a62-42a6-a920-191fb45242fb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=54d810a1&sv=2)

Unstake FET

[hashtag](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/kiln-products/dashboard/unstaking/fetch.ai-fet#re-delegate)

Re-delegate


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Re-delegating an FET stake can be useful when you wish to move your staked FET to a different validator without waiting for the 21 days unbonding period happening when unstaking.

This can be done by selecting "Re-delegate" for an FET stake on the dashboard and specifying a new validator.

![](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1911902555-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fnye3yqpuOzdfrtWAlwng%252Fuploads%252FhXYVDfVl320sB1fdnbSP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D99d8f986-e963-4bfd-a2fe-174bf293bce5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ebb84019&sv=2)

Redelegate FET

[hashtag](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/kiln-products/dashboard/unstaking/fetch.ai-fet#withdraw-rewards)

Withdraw rewards


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can withdraw your available FET rewards, by selecting "Withdraw rewards" on the dashboard. After that you will be able to connect your Fireblocks Vault and withdraw your FET rewards.

![](https://docs.kiln.fi/v1/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1911902555-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Fnye3yqpuOzdfrtWAlwng%252Fuploads%252FjombBzGHZlscqwwDOQa7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De0c3e2a9-f2dd-4940-abdd-d94b41e1e215&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4439c03a&sv=2)

Withdraw FET available rewards
